355.1(1): rigs/ chos lugs bcas gang la yang mthun sgril dang bde skyid kyi bkag rdo ru 'gyur

355.4(1): mkhas dbang mang pos yun ring re bskul byas pa'i rkyen dang / rgya che'i bod yig klog

356.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa

356.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas

356.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i
